April 2: (TW: flashing lights, spoilers in the intro video) Final Fantasy VI (commercial here) is released on the Super Famicom in Japan. The game was later re-released for the Final Fantasy Anthology compilation for the PlayStation in 1999, the Game Boy Advance in 2007, the Wii Virtual Console, and the iOS. This game was innovative for its steampunk-esque, Industrial Revolution setting instead of using the traditional medieval theme the JRPG was famous for at the time.
